 The Delhi High Court on Tuesday dismissed a petition by Ola, an app-based cab service provider
 mukhya nyaayadhish ji
 The bench of Rohini and Justice Jayant Nath dismissed Ola's plea
 yachika main ekal peeth ke 29 july ke ek aadesh ko chunauti di gai thi
 In a single bench order, the Delhi government and the traffic police were directed that a January order prohibiting radio cab services not registering under the Radio Taxi Scheme and using diesel fuel be strictly enforced
 dilli sarkaar ne radio taxi yojana 2006 ke dishanirdesh kaa paalan nahin karne vaali ap aadhaarit cab sevaaon par ek janvari ko roak laga di thi
 The guidelines of the Radio Taxi Scheme have been revised on 26 December 2014
 yachika main company ne yah tark pesh kiya tha ki ekal peeth ne sarvocch nyaayalay ke us aadesh ko najrandaaj kiya he, jisamen bataaya gaya he ki shahar main kisi prakaar kii texiyaan chalaai ja sakati hai
 The comments company ke vakil ne kaha ki sarvocch nyaayalay ne spasht kiya he ki usne euro-2 yaa usase behatar utsarjan maanakon kaa paalan karne vaali texiyon par roak nahin lagaai he
 It has also not ordered mandatory use of CNG
 company ne kaha ki sarvocch nyaayalay ne sirf yah kaha he ki dilli main 15 saal se adhik puraane vanijyik vaahanon kaa sanchaalan nahin kiya ja saktaa he
 He has not said anything about the fuel used therein
 ekal peeth ke aadesh main dilli sarkaar or yatayaat police ko yah nirdesh diya gaya tha ki radio taxi yojana main panjikaran nahin karaane vaali or dijal eendhan kaa upyog karne vaali radio cab sevaaon par roak lagane vaale ek janvari ke aadesh ko sakhti se lagu kiya jaae
 The Delhi government had on 1 January banned app-based cab services that did not follow the guidelines of the Radio Taxi Scheme 2006
 radio taxi yojana ke dishanirdesh ko 26 disambar, 2014 ko sanshodhit kiya gaya he
